British Prime Minister Accepts Invitation to Visit the United States Next Saturday with Experts 58

To Discuss Important International Issues

Roosevelt Declares Welcome

Reuter, London, 5th – British Prime Minister MacDonald has accepted President Roosevelt's invitation to visit Washington during the Easter period to discuss war debts and economic issues. London is now planning the meeting with the US President. It is learned today that the Prime Minister will leave the UK on April 15th, accompanied by his daughter and financial expert, Mr. Fu.

National, Washington, 5th – US President Roosevelt issued a statement today, stating that during this time when the UK and the US are informally exchanging views on the general economic situation and the war debt issue, he felt that the British Prime Minister's visit to Washington would be of great benefit. He solemnly expressed his hope that the British Prime Minister would come to the US for talks when he first met with British Ambassador Sir Lindsay at the hot springs. The public believes that this statement is sufficient to indicate that President Roosevelt had invited MacDonald to come to the US, but MacDonald had not yet notified the exact date of departure, and Roosevelt hoped that he would come to the US as soon as possible. Therefore, it is expected that a formal statement will be issued soon. The news that MacDonald will come to the US during the Easter holiday is because Congress will have a short recess during Easter, at which time the US government can concentrate on discussing everything with the British Prime Minister, so it is most appropriate for MacDonald to visit the US at this time. It is now speculated that after the British Prime Minister arrives in the US, the disarmament issue will also be discussed.

Keenly Desire France to Participate in Talks 59

Havas, Washington, 6th – President Roosevelt recently informed French Ambassador Claudel of British Prime Minister MacDonald's intention to come to the US as soon as possible, and said that he would be very happy if the US and France could hold talks at the same time. Roosevelt's intention seems to be that the future talks should be in the form of a conference of the three countries, the UK, France, and the US, which would be more appropriate. Although Roosevelt has not formally invited the French government to participate in the talks, he is willing to negotiate with French representatives on the preparations for the World Economic Conference, and then begin to discuss general political issues.

Davis Mediates Between France and Germany 60

National, Paris, 5th – Davis, the US representative to the Disarmament Conference, met with French Prime Minister Daladier today for more than an hour of in-depth discussions. All matters related to the Disarmament Conference and the Four-Power Pact were discussed. After the talks, Daladier immediately convened a cabinet meeting to report on the content of the talks with Davis. It is said that the French cabinet has decided to agree to the US proposal to convene a meeting of experts in Washington as a preliminary step to the future London World Economic Conference. The reason for France's agreement to this proposal is that France can first negotiate with the Washington authorities on the war debt issue when this preliminary meeting is convened.

National, Berlin, 6th – US Representative Davis is expected to arrive here on Saturday and Sunday to meet with Foreign Minister Neurath to discuss disarmament and the World Economic Conference.

Havas, Washington, 6th – Political circles believe that the visit of Davis, the chief representative to the Disarmament Conference, to Berlin is extremely important. They fear that Germany's reorganization of its armaments will cause the Disarmament Conference to fail. They hope that Davis can avoid this. This is the main task of Davis's trip to Europe. Generally, people also believe that economic truce, if Germany can cooperate, it will be of great value.

France Delays Submitting Memorandum on Four-Power Pact Plan 61

Still Insists on Opposing Revision of the Treaty

German Deputy Chancellor to Visit Rome

National, Paris, 6th – France's memorandum on the Four-Power Pact will not be submitted in Rome and London today. According to reports, the reason for the delay is due to opposition from French political circles to the entire plan. All newspapers say that France's memorandum only recognizes that the Four-Power Pact is a regional security agreement and must be included in the League of Nations Covenant. According to the Morning Post, the French government is willing to completely delete the revision of the treaty item from the agreement and replace it with a clause stipulating increased security and prohibiting Germany from re-establishing armaments.

Havas, Paris, 5th – The State Council met at the Presidential Palace today. Foreign Minister Poncet explained the French memorandum on the British-Italian Four-Power Pact plan, and the main part of it was approved by the State Council. This diplomatic note must be drafted at least two days later. After the State Council adjourned, government officials believed that Foreign Minister Poncet would explain the content of the diplomatic note when the House of Representatives discussed the budget.

Reuter, Berlin, 5th – Deputy Prime Minister von Papen and Speaker of the Reichstag Göring will go to Rome in the next few days to discuss disarmament issues and the Four-Power Pact with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. This news has been officially confirmed today.

National, Berlin, 5th – According to news from the Berlin Daily News, German Deputy Prime Minister von Papen will go to Italy in the next few days to consult with the Pope in Rome on the cooperation between the Catholic Church and the German National Socialist Party. These conditions for reconciliation have been under negotiation between the two sides for a long time. Papen's trip is just to complete the final formalities. Furthermore, German Aviation Minister Göring will also go to Italy to meet with Italian Air Minister Balbo, or perhaps pay homage to Prime Minister Mussolini. Therefore, there are many speculations about the two's trip to Italy. It is said that their trip will be the prelude to a meeting between German Chancellor Hitler and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini.

Italian Party Rejects Deletion 62

Reuters, Rome, 5th - The Fascist headquarters council met for three hours today, and then issued a communique, stating that the basic principles of Prime Minister Mussolini's Four-Power Pact plan must be complete and not deleted. Only in this way can the necessary conditions for peace be created and can be fairly recognized by all parties concerned.

Representatives of the Little Entente to Go to London 63

Havas, Paris, 5th – Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu has been discussing the international situation with French dignitaries for several days and has now set off for London to visit Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Minister Simon, explaining the views of the Little Entente countries on the Four-Power Pact plan.

US Large Navy Faction Advocates Actively Building Ships 64

Otherwise, Naval Power Will Be Ranked Fifth

National, Washington, 5th – US House Naval Committee Chairman Vinson stated in the committee today that the US Navy has fallen into a tragic situation. If it does not immediately start building ships, it will be reduced from its current third place in the world naval power to fifth place within three years. As for battleships alone, the United States will be on an equal footing with the United Kingdom. As for other important warships, the United States will be in fifth place by the end of 1936. For example, in terms of light cruisers, the United States will only have ten old ships by then. On the contrary, the United Kingdom will have twenty-one, Japan will have eighteen, and France and Italy will each have twelve. For example, in terms of destroyers, the United States will only have eleven ships by then, while the United Kingdom will have sixty-five, Japan sixty-seven, France fifty-eight, and Italy forty-eight. For example, the submarines that the United States currently has are rapidly becoming old. By 1936, there will only be twenty old ships. On the contrary, the United Kingdom will have thirty-nine, Japan eighty-one, France fifty-four, and Italy forty-seven. Although Vinson has always been known as a large navy faction, most of the committee members agree with this view. Therefore, the committee has decided today to immediately begin a detailed study of the need for shipbuilding and has invited Navy Chief of Staff Swanson to discuss this matter with the committees tomorrow. Vinson also stated that while the US Navy's strength is diminishing due to not building new ships permitted by the treaty, discussing disarmament with the great powers is of little value. Because the United States' failure to build new ships is equivalent to actual disarmament, it is difficult to discuss further reductions.

British Restriction on Russian Goods Case 65

Passed Second Reading by Lower House

Havas, London, 6th – The bill on restricting the import of Russian goods has been passed by the House of Commons in the second reading by 347 votes to 48.

Dispute over Eastern Greenland 66

The Hague Court Rules in Favor of Norway

Reuter, The Hague, 5th – Denmark and Norway have been unable to resolve their dispute over certain parts of Eastern Greenland, so they have asked the Permanent Court of International Justice in The Hague to adjudicate. Today, the court ruled in favor of Denmark by twelve votes to two. When the two countries submitted the case, they stated that they would accept the court's verdict without reservation. The cause of the dispute was that a Norwegian private hunting team landed in Eastern Greenland, raised the Norwegian flag there, and recognized that part of the land belonged to Norway. The Norwegian government later formally recognized this move. The Hague Court has now determined that Norway's occupation of the land violates current law, so it ruled that the land should still belong to Denmark.

National, Oslo, 5th – Norwegian Prime Minister Mowinckel told a news reporter today that Norway has submitted the Eastern Greenland case to the International Court of Justice, and now that the court has ruled in favor of Denmark, the Norwegian government will naturally obey in order to maintain close friendship with the Danish people. He also said that Denmark's economic interests in Eastern Greenland are guaranteed by the 1924 Danish-Norwegian treaty, which will not expire until 1944.

Bill to Prohibit Publication of Secret Documents 67

US Senate Requests Government Explanation

National, Washington, 5th – Today, the US Senate Foreign Relations Committee invited representatives from the State Department and the Department of Justice to attend a meeting to explain the reasons for requesting the enactment of a bill to prohibit the publication of government secret documents. This request was made by the State Department and no explanation was given at the time. Although it has now been hastily passed by both houses of Congress, the Senate was surprised to learn that this case was advocated by Secretary of State Hull personally. Moreover, those who advocated the passage of this case at the time expected that the government's goal was to prohibit the publication of Jett Lauck's book on Japanese diplomatic secrets. However, according to what was heard today, the State Department's move was not solely for this book, so it wants to ask the two departments to explain. However, all committee members believe that in such matters, especially when there is a need to enact laws, the State Department should be absolutely trusted, so their request for an explanation is only to hear the truth and has no other opinions. When the representatives of the two departments attend the meeting to explain, a closed-door meeting will be held to maintain confidentiality. Although Secretary of State Hull said that Congress should legislate to protect US secret codes, there is no claim that US codebooks have been stolen.

Roosevelt Reaffirms Gold Hoarding Ban 68

National Finance Still Not Out of Emergency State

National, Washington, 5th – The US President issued an executive order today, declaring that the national finance has not yet emerged from the emergency state, and all emergency orders and regulations are still valid. He also reaffirmed the order prohibiting the hoarding of gold coins, bullion, and gold securities, except for those specifically exempted. Those who have gold must send it to the Federal Reserve Bank or its agent before May 1. The gold coins or gold securities that each person keeps for personal use must not exceed one hundred yuan. However, gold legally used for industrial purposes does not need to be handed over, and gold coins collected by antique collectors are also exempt, but only those collected as antiques. Gold coins marked as owned by foreign governments and banks and gold coins approved for transportation are also exempt.

Gold Export Restrictions May Be Relaxed Slightly 69

National, New York, 5th – The National Chamber of Commerce has been investigating the financial situation for a long time, and several of its suggestions have been adopted by the US President, so it occupies a significant position in the US financial policy. Tonight, it also suggested that foreign exchange restrictions should be lifted, as long as it does not conflict with gold export restrictions. It said that it is now necessary to restore the free exchange of gold pounds and other foreign currencies. If this measure is not enough to promote the progress of business, then the value of the US gold dollar will have to be reduced so that foreign countries can buy gold dollars at a lower cost to buy US goods. The committee includes many well-known figures in the business and financial world, such as Rosenwald, Ping Dix, and Rand. They previously suggested banning the transportation of gold and stopping the payment of currency. They still suggest continuing to ban the transportation of gold until the UK and the US can hold a joint meeting to discuss this matter and advocate that efforts to maintain the full price of the gold dollar can be stopped. The joint meeting between the UK and the US should aim at restoring the true gold standard at the same time.

Havas, Washington, 6th – Secretary of the Treasury Woodin recently convened a meeting of seventeen senators and representatives from states related to the silver issue. After the meeting, he told reporters that he had decided to thoroughly study all methods of raising the price of silver before making a decision.

Havas, Washington, 6th – President Roosevelt has signed an order stipulating that beer sales events will simultaneously begin to issue sales licenses. The first license was obtained by the American Press Club. Beer sales have been deemed legal in Washington and nineteen other states starting from midnight on Friday. US Navy Commander-in-Chief to Thoroughly Investigate Cause of Zeppelin Disaster 72

National News Agency, Washington, 5th - Today, US Navy Commander-in-Chief Byrd stated that he will begin a thorough investigation of the Akron zeppelin disaster at Lakehurst on Monday morning. When the zeppelin crashed in the storm, Rear Admiral Wiley, who was in charge of the ship, visited Navy Chief of Staff Swanson today to describe the situation in detail. Afterwards, Swanson and Byrd agreed on the date of the thorough investigation.

Since the zeppelin accident, public opinion across the country has been demanding a thorough investigation. Byrd and Swanson have agreed to thoroughly investigate the case and will publish all the details. The chief investigator will be Rear Admiral Phillips, assisted by Colonel Hume, commander of the Sunnyvale Naval Air Station in California, and Major Horton, commander of the lighter-than-air aviation unit. The investigation will be as thorough as possible to satisfy public demand. Naval authorities, having heard news that fragments of zeppelin wreckage were floating in the ocean near the accident site, dispatched ships again today to search for them in the hope of finding something that could be used to discover the weaknesses in the zeppelin's construction. However, nothing had been found by late at night.

Preparations for Japan's Total War Mobilization (Continued from Part 3) 75

9. Industrial Mobilization and Peacetime Surveys

The survey on industrial mobilization is the responsibility of the Military Demand Survey Committee or the Resource Survey Committee. For many factories, wartime conditions are planned, and they are ordered to conduct surveys from peacetime. Once war breaks out, the first thing is to make these factories immediately engage in the manufacture of military supplies. However, it must be noted here that Japan's industries are mostly biased towards the textile industry and the food industry, while the metal industry, machinery and equipment industry, and chemical industry, which are necessary for the military industry, are relatively sluggish. This is a shortcoming.

Regarding the method of conducting industrial mobilization, if we examine the cases submitted to the parliament since the European War, we seem to be able to divide it into two systems. One is that the government itself does not manage the military supply manufacturing factories, but entrusts it to groups or companies. The other is the method by which the government directly manages the factories. The former is the method adopted by Germany during the Great War, and the latter is the method that France and Italy wanted to carry out or are carrying out after the war. Japan's industrial mobilization law also uses the government's power to manage, use, or requisition factories, so it belongs to the latter.

The requisition of transportation agencies is to be done according to the requisition order. The requisition of transportation agencies is not entirely for industrial mobilization. If it is for military use, the military will requisition it and the military will use it. However, there is a kind of protection car that should be requisitioned according to the Military Protection Car Law and a certain amount of compensation should be paid.

In Germany, it is often heard that the chairs in Berlin parks disappear immediately whenever a war breaks out and are eventually moved into trucks for transporting soldiers. Because there is a budget in advance, the length of the chairs has been decided long ago. And in order to accommodate the war-wounded, there were not enough beds in the train, so benches were used instead. This was also planned in advance. Like this, in order to carry out total mobilization, one should focus on peacetime facilities.

Now the National Defense Women's Association is also gradually becoming popular throughout the country. Each member usually wears a gold ring as a sign of membership. Once the country is in a state of emergency, they must take off their gold rings and donate them to the country. Paper money rises and falls irregularly due to the current price, but gold rings are stable. Such a plan is now underway, so Japanese women each carry a gold ring, and once there is a war, it can immediately increase by hundreds of millions of yuan. This is now being promoted very well. Now, in the Kansai area, the coats, clothes, and hats worn by teachers and students are similar in material to those worn by the military. This is the uniform of schools in the Kyoto area, and it has also been extended to the Osaka area. This is being carried out from the perspective of national total mobilization. In the Osaka clothing factory, you can see the organization of the Clothing Association. Of course, there are soldiers participating in this. Woolen fabric operators and dye operators are all participating. The obvious achievement is that the private sector has continuously produced gray-quality clothing. Even if these things are not carried out for total mobilization, the result is also a kind of peacetime facility for total mobilization. Once a war breaks out, it will be useful immediately. Even if it becomes the cultivation of clothing resources, from the perspective of total mobilization, it can be said that the Clothing Association is carrying out the work of total mobilization. Such things seem to be seen everywhere since the September 18th Incident.

If such things are actively carried out in the mobilization plan, this is a help for the national consensus towards improving national defense power, and it is also a kind of peacetime facility for national total mobilization.

Also, the shape of the cans has also become a certain size for army use. A certain canning company in Hokkaido seems to have completely changed it to a military style.

10. Japan's Lack of Self-Sufficiency

Speaking of Japan's ability to have self-sufficient national power, it must go through a considerable amount of time. So, in the current state of Japan, once a war starts, there is no ability to be self-sufficient immediately. This path of self-sufficiency is now underway. If a war starts now, the first thing we immediately feel is the lack of oil. Although we also have oil fields in Manchuria and Sakhalin that can be developed, other important resources for national defense can also be supplied from Manchuria. However, oil cannot be obtained immediately after it is mined, so the current state of Japan cannot be self-sufficient no matter what. The most felt is the lack of oil. How to enable oil to be self-sufficient to some extent in the country is a big problem. Now, a lot of oil is imported from the United States. If it can be continuously imported from the United States as usual, then there is no problem. If we encounter a situation where we cannot rely on the United States, we must think of another way. In addition, we can also rely on oil from the South Seas or Russia, or find a way to import it from Europe. However, the feasibility of its implementation only depends on our careful planning and peacetime preparation. Otherwise, it is very difficult in practice.

11. Is Japan's War Expenditure Sufficient?

However, on the one hand, the most worrying thing is the issue of money for using resources. This is about the question of how much money will be needed for the future war. In total, 500 to 600 million is needed a year. If it continues for two years, 100 to 100 million is needed. This is only the number needed by the army. The country must need more. However, looking at past wars, the issue of war expenditure, an increase in taxes is only a part of the war expenditure. The main force of war expenditure should be based on public bonds and non-convertible paper money. The problem of money is not a problem if we win the war. If we lose the war, it is terrible. Germany lost, and one trillion marks plummeted to five cents. If Japan loses the war, it will be terrible. Every Japanese citizen believes that the difficulty when a war starts is the problem of resources, and especially the difficulty is money.

The Tragic State of Jianchang Camp After the Japanese Plane Bombing 76

Each Bomb Weighed Over 240 Pounds

No Land Intact Within the City, Many Deaths

Refugees Claim Japanese Soldiers Committed Rape and Murder at Will

A Tangshan dispatch: Yang Letian, an executive member of the Tangshan City Party Department, returned yesterday from Qian'an. He spoke of the devastating bombing by Japanese planes in the Lengkou Jianchang Camp area, a situation too terrible to bear. The following is a record of Yang's account:

"Currently, at Xifengkou North and various other passes, the enemy and our troops are confronting each other both inside and outside the passes. However, Dongjiakou, east of Xifengkou, is now occupied by the enemy.

The [missing characters] army units are mostly stationed in the Xiaojiaying and Madaogou areas, more than twenty miles outside Lengkou, constructing strong defensive works and maintaining strict vigilance. They are also facing each other. Both enemy and our positions are on the mountains, but the enemy's mountain is higher than ours. They constantly shoot at us with machine guns. Our soldiers have high morale and ignore the enemy's aimless firing. They wait for the enemy to get close, then launch fierce attacks with broadswords and hand grenades. Every attack hits its mark, and every swing of the sword finds its target. Enemy planes constantly drop bombs on various villages inside and outside Lengkou, causing great damage. Jianchang Camp was the most severely bombed, with hardly any land intact within the city. Judging from the extent of the explosions, the bombs weighed over 240 pounds each. For example, a bomb dropped in front of the Yuqingyong store on East Street not only destroyed the building and created a large crater, but also blasted a two-foot square flagstone into the air, landing it on the roof of a house on the north side of the street. The soil blasted from the crater could level the surrounding buildings, and after the buildings next to the crater were bombed a second time and collapsed into the crater, the crater was still over ten feet deep. The cruelty of the Japanese is unmatched. A bomb dropped inside the Catholic Church on North Street killed two people, including a priest, it is said. Four people died in the east neighbor, and two people died in the west neighbor. The Shunxing store on West Street was also hit by a bomb, killing and injuring one person each, and also killing a donkey. One person was killed at the Little West Gate. The Yuan Rong residence in Xiguan was bombed, killing two men and one woman. The fate of the children is unknown. The Yuqingyong, Yongshenglong, Fuji, Yong Sheng He, and Xu Zhang residences on East Street were all hit by multiple bombs, and the casualties are unclear. The Zhao Family Inn, Haiji Pawnshop, Li Residence on South Street, as well as the houses on both sides of the city wall and gate in Nanguan, were all destroyed by bombs. Three houses were destroyed in Wang Family Shop in Nanguan, with no trace of bricks and tiles, only a large crater.

Currently, the residents of Jianchang Camp have all fled. It is said that although there has been no detailed investigation of the number of people killed by the bombing, it is known that there are already more than thirty people. On the 30th of last month, eleven enemy planes bombed Baiyangluokou on a large scale. The extent of the bombing is currently unknown.

According to refugees who escaped from Dushan, there are many Mongolians and Koreans in the Japanese army, but few Chinese. Several are translators. The Japanese are extremely cruel to the Chinese. Once Chinese land is occupied, they want to kill all intellectuals to eliminate future troubles. Therefore, whenever they encounter men with long robes and delicate hands, resembling literate men, they kill them without asking questions. Whenever they see people with rough clothes and dirty faces, short, hard fingers, and braids hanging down their backs, the Japanese always say "Good, good." As for women, their suffering is beyond words. It is not easy to endure humiliation and survive, and it is difficult to seek death. The Japanese openly commit rape, and almost all women are humiliated. They also occasionally give small favors to the villagers to win their hearts. They forcibly search and burn books in schools and civilian homes.

The Japanese rely entirely on modern weapons to fight against us. In fact, the Japanese soldiers have very little courage and are most afraid of our army's broadswords. They say that if they are killed by broadswords, they cannot be reincarnated as human beings in the next life. Therefore, everyone wears two or three amulets to ensure they will not die or be reborn as human beings after death. Their cowardice and ignorance prove the extreme wickedness of the Japanese warlords. The text on their amulets reads "戸户神社 (May martial luck last forever) Amulet" and "天津日高彦火歹出見命御守". The character "神" (God) in the former and the characters "高彦" (Takihiko) in the latter both have red seals stamped on them, but the characters are unclear. The characters on the amulets are also very neatly written." (April 2nd)

The 19th Route Army's Anti-Japanese Troops Are Organized 77

Soldiers Selected by Drawing Lots

Those Selected Rejoice, Those Not Selected Are Disappointed

A Fuzhou dispatch: Cai Tingkai, Commander-in-Chief of the 19th Route Army, flew from the province to Zhangzhou on the afternoon of March 30th to prepare for sending troops to aid Rehe. Zhang Yan and Tan Qixiu had previously been rumored to be appointed as commanders of the aid-Rehe army columns and had already gone to Guangdong to make arrangements. As for the 19th Route Army's plan to send troops, it was originally planned to select twelve people from each company to form [missing character] regiment. Soldiers who volunteered to go filled out application forms and waited to be selected. However, after this order was issued, soldiers competed to go, and some entire companies even submitted applications, making it impossible for the regimental headquarters to select. Therefore, they decided to use drawing lots to decide. Those who were selected were all joyful and excited, while those who were not selected were very disappointed. The troops stationed in northern Fujian have now been fully selected and organized and are marching empty-handed to Zhangzhou to receive new, sharp firearms. They will join the troops selected in southern Fujian and go north to Guangdong. All sectors of Yong'an specially held a large meeting the other day to bid them farewell and presented them with a satin banner that read "Kill the Enemy for the Country" as a memento. At that time, a soldier representing the entire group took the stage and gave a speech that was extremely tragic. He said that they would go with the determination to die without returning and fight the enemy to the end. He only hoped that those who followed could step on the heads and blood of those who went before and advance forward, and that they would not look back until they had achieved the goal of recovering lost territory. The audience was deeply moved. In addition to holding a large anti-Japanese national salvation donation drive from the 1st to the 3rd, raising funds to purchase items for comfort, the male and female students of the normal and vocational middle schools in Fuzhou also launched the organization of an ambulance team. The various procedures have now been roughly prepared, and they are scheduled to go to Zhangzhou after the spring vacation and depart with the army. In addition, the Pacification Headquarters had previously issued a notice to the counties to raise and transport teams. Now, more than 1,900 people have been sent from the counties and will be divided into 36 classes, exclusively for bandit suppression. Outside rumors that they will also go north with the army are not true. Regarding the news of bandit suppression on the Fujian border, after the bandit army in Changting was attacked by the three divisions of Qu Shounian, Shen Guanghan, and Huang Renhuan, divided from Liancheng, Shanghang, and Nanyang, their situation became increasingly desperate. Now, only Li Shaozhou's false independent regiment remains in Ting City, and the rest have fled back to Ruijin. (April 3rd)

Local News

Abolishing the Taels and Changing to Yuan Implemented Yesterday 89

Silver and Money Industries Resolved Methods for Internal and External Dealings

Foreign Banks Receive and Deliver Silver Dollars for Chinese Merchants

The Taels-Yuan Exchange Management Committee Has Been Ordered to Be Abolished

But Those Holding Silver Are Still Allowed to Exchange at Three Banks

An order from the Ministry of Finance states that, starting yesterday, all public and private funds and transactions must be converted to silver dollars, and taels may no longer be used. The silver and money industries held separate member meetings to resolve compliance. A temporary joint meeting of foreign banks decided on methods. The Taels-Yuan Exchange Management Committee, jointly formed by the three banks, has been ordered to be abolished and will be handled by the Central, etc., Three Banks, only allowing the exchange of silver for silver dollars. The exchange of silver and money industry silver notes has been abolished. The details are as follows:

Resolutions of the Money Industry Association 90

The Money Industry Association held a temporary emergency member representative meeting at 8:30 PM the night before last, chaired by Qin Runqing. Six items for handling external and internal matters were resolved: (1) Accounts with business clients will be settled with interest as of April 5th, and transferred at a rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar. The deposit interest will be deducted at 2 taels and 95 hundredths, and debts will be added; (2) Remittances between peers will be received and delivered in silver dollars; (3) Various notes, checks, and drafts will be settled at 715 thousandths of a silver dollar; (5) Notes received from external banks on the same day must be in silver dollars. If paying with banknotes, the amount must not exceed 500 yuan; (6) Long-term deposits will be annotated with the number of silver dollars converted at a rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar for each transaction and will be combined at the end of the year, and this will be announced in the newspaper. The association has received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance stating: (excerpt omitted). The implementation methods were then assigned: (1) All kinds of silver notes issued before April 6th should be paid at a rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar; (2) Starting from April 6th, all kinds of notes should be denominated in silver dollars. If silver taels are still used, customers should be asked to convert to silver dollars before payment; (3) Starting from April 6th, all silver tael deposits and debts in various accounts should be transferred to silver dollars at the legal rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar. This special announcement is hereby made in the newspaper for your reference.

Resolutions of the Banking Association 91

In addition to holding a member meeting the night before last and announcing three methods in the newspaper, the Banking Association held another member meeting at 11:00 AM yesterday, chaired by Li Fuxun. It was resolved that: (1) The three banks' exchange agency will continue to operate, but only allowing the exchange of silver for silver dollars, and the time will be extended; (2) If banks and money shops receive silver tael checks from foreign banks, the receiving bank or money shop should endorse the check and write "This check is only allowed to be exchanged for silver dollars at the Central, China, and Communications Banks" before entering it into the silver dollar account; (3) Silver tael notes of foreign banks must be exchanged for silver dollar notes at the legal rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar before they can be used for payment; (4) Term notes that mature before April 15th may be paid at a rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar. If the maturity date is after April 15th, they should be registered with the association before April 15th, and the payment will be made at a rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar upon maturity; (5) All foreign exchange transactions should be received and paid with silver dollar notes. Items 2, 3, 4, and 5 will be submitted by both associations to the Ministry of Finance and forwarded to the judicial authorities for record.

Meeting of Foreign Banks 92

Foreign banks held a joint meeting at the Chartered Bank on the Bund at 4:00 PM yesterday. Representatives from HSBC, Chartered, Citibank, Banque de l'Indochine, Yokohama Specie Bank, Mitsui Bank, Bank of Taiwan, and Banque Belge pour l'Étranger attended. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM. A reporter from the New Sound Society visited a deputy comprador of the Chartered Bank last night. According to him, the joint meeting of foreign banks resolved two items: (1) The receipt and delivery of silver taels and silver dollars between foreign banks will continue as before; (2) The receipt and delivery of silver taels from Chinese banks and money shops will be calculated in silver dollars.

Foreign Merchants Temporarily Continue to Use Silver 93

The Shanghai Evening Post & Mercury reports that the Ministry of Finance's telegram ordering the implementation of abolishing taels and changing to yuan today (6th) should, in theory, be binding on all foreign banks. However, according to a Mr. from the American Far East Bank this morning, foreign banks will temporarily continue to use silver. Foreign bankers initially did not expect the silver dollar to become the sole legal tender so quickly. They were shocked by the sudden implementation of abolishing taels in one night. Therefore, they will temporarily continue to use silver taels for transactions.

All Industries Implement Abolishing Taels 94

After the silver and money industries were ordered to implement abolishing taels and changing to yuan, the banks and money shops yesterday stopped issuing silver tael notes. All silver tael notes issued before April 6th were annotated on the back with the amount of silver dollars converted at a rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar upon receipt and delivery. All silver tael calculations for various business clients were converted to silver dollars. The receipt and delivery of silver taels from foreign banks was changed to be calculated in silver dollars. Starting today, the Banking Association will handle the registration of long-term silver tael notes that mature after April 15th. As for foreign exchange transactions, silver dollar notes will be used for receipt and payment.

Abolishing Silver Note Exchange 95

The Preparatory Committee of the Joint Association of Banking Associations issued a notice yesterday: "To whom it may concern, the Banking Association of this city received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance today stating that, starting April 6th, all public and private funds, contracts, notes, and transactions must be converted to silver dollars and silver taels may no longer be used. The association has immediately resolved three implementation methods and sent them for publication in the newspaper. Based on the above regulations, this association has decided that: (1) The exchange of silver taels and silver tael drafts by this association will be abolished starting April 6th; (2) Starting April 6th, for silver taels and silver tael drafts received by the exchange bank that were issued before April 6th, each note should be converted into silver dollars and silver dollar drafts at the legal rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar, and the converted amount should be indicated on the note in red numbers before being presented for exchange; (3) If there are silver tael and silver tael draft accounts with business clients of the exchange bank, this association will transfer them to silver dollar and silver dollar draft accounts at the legal rate of 715 thousandths of a silver dollar on April 6th. In addition to notifying the exchange, this notice is hereby sent to you for your information. The Money Industry Association's interbank single (i.e., note exchange) will abolish silver tael singles and only handle silver dollar singles starting yesterday.

Abolishing the Exchange Management Committee 96

The Silver Taels and Silver Dollars Exchange Management Committee, jointly formed by the Central, China, and Communications Banks under the order of the Ministry of Finance, was established on March 10th and began operations. Yesterday, it received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance: "To the Silver Taels and Silver Dollars Exchange Management Committee: This ministry has decided that, starting April 6th, all public and private funds and transactions must be converted to silver dollars and silver taels may no longer be used. As for the exchange of silver taels and silver dollars, it is no longer necessary to continue operations. You are hereby ordered to abolish and cease the exchange operations immediately. Minister of Finance Song Ziwen." After receiving the order, the committee immediately proceeded with the closure. The attached office of the Central Bank has ceased the exchange operations since yesterday.

The Central Government Will Never Compromise with Japan 97

Song Ziwen Talks

My Resignation as President of the Central Bank is an Active Assumption of Responsibility

The Ministry of Finance Coordinates the Overall Situation and Strives for Economic Construction

The Foundation of the Central Bank is Solid and Can Be Further Developed

丨Song Visited Kong Yesterday Morning to Urge Him to Serve as President, But Kong Firmly Declined丨

Song Ziwen, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, left Nanjing by overnight train the night before last and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning. He immediately returned to his private residence on Route Américan and went to the Shanghai office to work. At around 9:00 AM, Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Mao Bangchu, Principal of the Aviation School, visited him one after another. At 11:00 AM, Song visited Kong Xiangxi to urge him to serve as President of the Central Bank and share the arduous task. Kong politely declined, telling reporters that he was not qualified for the job and would definitely not accept it. The following is a record of the speeches of the two:

Song's Speech 98

Active Responsibility: There have been rumors recently that someone in charge of military affairs is unwilling to expand military operations against Japan, so Song has expressed negativity and is tired of his duties. A reporter from the New Sound Society specially visited Song at 10:00 AM this morning to inquire about the matter. Song replied that there was no such thing. The origin of this rumor must be due to the speculation surrounding my resignation as President of the Central Bank. In fact, my resignation as President of the Central Bank is precisely to actively assume responsibility. There are three reasons:

The Foundation is Solid: In the early days of the Central Bank's establishment, due to the initial organization and the unsteady foundation, the Minister of Finance had to serve concurrently. Over the years, it has gone through major and dangerous environments such as internal strife, floods, foreign humiliation, and falling silver prices, but the Central Bank has remained unaffected. Now the foundation is very solid, and business development no longer needs to be handled by me concurrently. This is one reason. Overall Consideration: As Minister of Finance, in terms of my responsibilities, I should take into account the maintenance and adjustment of the national financial economy as a whole. Serving concurrently as President of the Central Bank would create the appearance of favoring one bank and neglecting the overall situation, which is inconvenient. This is the second reason.

Economic Construction: The most important thing in finance today is to plan wartime military spending, but economic construction cannot be ignored. The economy is the foundation of the country, and our country's current situation is very immature and backward. If we do not catch up quickly and only make plans for stopgap measures, there will inevitably be a day when we run out of resources. I plan to devote myself to this in the future, but the organization of the Central Bank is becoming increasingly complex, and it is difficult to take care of both. This is the third reason.

Maintaining the Status Quo: Based on these three reasons, after I resigned as President of the Central Bank, President Wang recommended former Minister Kong to succeed me. There have been no changes to the supervisors of the Central Bank, and all policies will remain the same. In the future, the Ministry of Finance will, of course, fulfill its full responsibility for maintaining the Central Bank and achieve the effect of working together. With someone in charge, it can be further developed.

No Compromise: As for Chiang Kai-shek's trip to Nanchang, it was because the communist bandits in Jiangxi Province were rampant that he had to go there personally, and it was definitely not to relax the war in North China. Rumors that someone advocated compromise are pure speculation. I repeat this to make it clear. No one in the government or the central government is willing to be a Li Hongzhang. Other political issues are not for me to express, as I have already resigned from my position in the Executive Yuan. According to customs news, there is fighting five miles north of Qinhuangdao in the North China war.

Kong's Speech 99

Expressing His Refusal: Kong Xiangxi told a reporter from the Central News Agency after meeting with Minister Song that Minister Song had resigned from his position as President of the Central Bank due to busy schedules, and the Central Political Conference had resolved to appoint him as his successor. However, I have not yet received a formal order, so I cannot express whether or not I will accept the position. Taking a step back, even if the central government formally appoints me as the president of the bank, I will definitely refuse to accept the position. The Central Bank is a national bank, and its scale is huge. Only those with scholarship and experience like Minister Song can be competent. I have shallow scholarship and lack experience in managing banks. I feel that I am not competent for this important national financial institution. When I was Minister of Industry in the past, I founded the National Goods Bank, but the National Goods Bank was smaller in scale and easier to manage, which is different from this. At this time of national crisis and China's financial recession, all Chinese people should share the arduous task, but one must know that those who are skilled in craftsmanship are not good at farming, and those who are farmers are not good at being merchants. If one tries to force oneself, one will not be able to do it. Therefore, my expression of not accepting the position is just this meaning.

Song Zheyuan's Representative Reports on the Bloody Battle at Xifengkou 100

Receiving the Press at the YMCA Yesterday Afternoon

All the Officers and Soldiers of the Army Hold the Determination Not to Retreat Until Death

Hope that the National Army Will Rise Up to Recover Lost Territory

Xiao Zhenying, the representative of Song Zheyuan, the Commander-in-Chief of the Third Army Group and concurrently the Commander of the Twenty-Ninth Army, accompanied by Sun Longji, the representative of the army stationed in Shanghai, received the local press at the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA at twelve o'clock yesterday afternoon, reporting on the army's battle against the enemy at Xifengkou. More than forty reporters from various newspapers attended. Xiao and Sun detailed the desperate battle against the enemy, which was so passionate and tragic that all the reporters were moved. The details are recorded separately below.

The Big Sword for Slaying Enemies 101

Yesterday afternoon, after the reporters arrived one after another, Mr. Xiao and Mr. Sun, the two representatives, displayed three types of photographs of war trophies from the victory of their army at Xifengkou, as well as a diagram depicting the army's flanking maneuver to encircle and kill the enemy. The photos included steel armored vehicles, Junkers aircraft, military flags, military caps, and more. Subsequently, they displayed a large sword used for killing enemies, with fresh bloodstains on it. They stated that this sword had already killed more than ten enemies on the front lines. When Mr. Kong Xiangxi visited Xifengkou previously, he specially brought it to Shanghai as a memento. In addition, there were more than ten absurd proclamations from the enemy's command headquarters, and two satirical drawings.

A Detailed Account of the Bloody Battle 102

During the gathering, Mr. Xiao Zhenying, the representative, first reported, "Our army's actions in killing the enemy at Xifengkou were truly the duty of soldiers, and not worthy of praise. However, we are grateful for the encouragement of national public opinion and the added support from all sides. We would like to express our deepest gratitude. To ensure that all sectors understand the overall situation of this defensive battle, we are taking advantage of today's gathering to provide some supplementary details. In today's world, the tools of war are becoming increasingly scientific. Aircraft and cannons are the tools of victory. Our army, lacking equipment, wants to compete with others. We feel that flesh and blood cannot be 'scientified,' and our hands and feet cannot be turned into cannonballs. Thinking about this, the situation is indeed vastly different, and we would be defeated before the battle even begins. How can we talk about resistance? But the reality is not entirely so. Based on the experience gained from our army's battle, we know that victory does not depend entirely on sophisticated weapons and equipment. It is only when the spirit is strong that the battle can be won." At this point, Mr. Xiao produced a battle map of Xifengkou and hung it on the wall, continuing to describe the situation of the bloody battle at the time. "When the Northeast Army began to withdraw on March 8th, it had withdrawn to Xifengkou by the 9th. The Japanese army followed closely behind, arriving at Xifengkou within three hours. At that time, Army Commander Song was stationed in Zunhua, sixty miles east of Xifengkou. The Japanese army arrived successively and occupied the high mountain positions in and outside of Xifengkou, placing eighteen cannons at Heishan Mouth. Our army rushed to support at a rate of twenty miles per hour. The Japanese army, positioned high above, bombarded us with artillery fire. The two companies of our army's vanguard were completely wiped out. Two more companies were sent forward, but only a dozen or so survived. At the same time, Brigade Commander Zhao used the telephone to ask Army Commander Song for instructions. Song believed that if Xifengkou was lost, Tianjin and Beijing would be in danger. He repeatedly ordered that they advance without retreat, and fight to the death. He personally went to the front line to supervise the battle. After three days and nights of bloody fighting, our army had suffered 2,000 casualties due to the terrain. A cadre meeting was then convened. Army Commander Song said that the enemy occupied superior geographical positions, making it very difficult to attack. We would have to resort to unconventional tactics to win. Therefore, it was decided to implement a large-scale encirclement, dispatching Brigade Commanders Zhao Dengyu, Wang Zhibang, and Tong Zeguang to divide their troops into three routes, encircling the rear of the enemy. At that time, Brigade Commander Zhao had not fully recovered from his leg injury, and many advised him not to go. Zhao jumped out of bed and declared, 'Now is the time for men to serve their country! Why hesitate?' He advanced despite his injury. Overnight, they completely surrounded the enemy. It was at night, with close-quarters combat. The enemy could not distinguish between reality and illusion, and they killed each other, collapsing without forming ranks. In this battle, all the enemy units stationed from Xifengkou to Hengcheng to Baozi, and north to Langdongzi, were annihilated, totaling about 10,000 men. When the fighting was intense, more than sixty civilians acted as guides, burning all of the enemy's supply train at Caijia Ridge, so that the fire lit up the sky. The surrounded enemy then recognized the truth. When they tried to bombard our position with artillery, our army had already changed the enemy's position into our own. In this battle, Brigade Commander Zhao Dengyu and Regiment Commander Li Zenzhong were the bravest, advancing despite their injuries, so they could inspire the morale and achieve this success. If Brigade Commander Wang Zhibang had not arrived an hour late due to the distance, and if it were not for the fire at Caijia Ridge, our army would have followed the advance directly to Chengde. Now our army's position is secure, and there are no enemy traces fifty miles away. The Japanese army is indeed afraid of the bravery of our big sword teams."

Soldiers Should Sacrifice 103

Before the whole army resisted, Army Commander Song had instructed the soldiers, "Our country now has no other way out except to resist and sacrifice. And those who should first resolve to sacrifice are our soldiers. Japan's strength came from the Russo-Japanese War. In one battle, they advanced to occupy a ridge, sacrificing more than 5,000 men. If Japan had not made sacrifices at that time, how could it have the strength of today, and further invade our China? At that time, the disparity in strength between Japan and Russia was vast, but Japan won by fighting to the death and sacrificing. Therefore, our country's soldiers, at this time, should also fight to the death to the end. If there is one soldier left, we will never retreat, to avenge the entire nation and be the first to advocate for all the country's soldiers." At that time, the soldiers all unanimously expressed their willingness to kill the enemy and sacrifice. He continued, "Our army is hosting you today, not to boast about the battle, nor to flaunt the success of a single battle. The purpose is to hope that you can advise all the country's soldiers. From the Shanghai War and the Xifengkou War, we can see that the Japanese army relies only on aircraft, cannons, and other sophisticated weapons. But their strength can only extend to destruction. In true close-quarters combat, the Japanese army is actually inferior to us. As long as the country's soldiers can prepare to sacrifice, they will surely be able to avenge the national shame and recover the lost territories."

Report by Representative Sun 104

After Mr. Xiao's report, Mr. Sun Longji, the representative of Mr. Song, also reported on the army's sincere attitude towards defending the country, saying that after the Japanese occupied Shenyang on September 18th, the people of the whole country believed that the Japanese army was strong and that it would be difficult for us to resist in any way. However, since the Shanghai War on January 28th, our 19th Route Army resisted the Japanese with sincerity, repeatedly defeating strong enemies, sweeping away the previous demoralization. The soldiers of the whole country have also realized that as long as they resist desperately, they can destroy the tyranny. Army Commander Song has been advocating for active resistance. When the 19th Route Army was carrying out the war of resistance in Shanghai, Mr. Song specially sent four senior staff officers to Shanghai to inspect. Based on the experience gained from the inspection, they trained the soldiers. Therefore, in this battle, all the soldiers of our army were inspired to resist the enemy's strong weapons with our flesh and blood, and finally recovered the lost Xifengkou, ensuring the safety of the gateway to North China. Up to now, there are no enemy traces fifty miles away, and our army also goes on the offensive from time to time. In this battle, our army gained a lot. Just for machine guns, we have more than a thousand. Other items such as cannons are even harder to count. When the news of the victory came out, the British, American, and French embassies in China all sent military attachés to inspect. They were impressed by the bravery of our army, but also felt confused. Our army's chief of staff explained the truth of the battle, saying that the Japanese army's aircraft and cannons can only be used for destruction and long-range trench warfare. In close-quarters combat, they completely lose their effectiveness. Our army uses broadswords in combat. Although machine guns are like a string of pearls, they still have a chance to rest. Our army takes advantage of this to send one or two people to the front line. The enemy is cut down by the broadswords, and the machine guns are seized by us, ultimately winning the final victory. Currently, our army is firmly guarding the front line. Soldiers and officers are all determined to sacrifice, and we will never give up an inch of land. Hosting you today is not to boast about the victory, but just to briefly report the truth, so that the country's soldiers can rise up and recover the lost territories.

Talk by Li Weishi, American Advisor to the Chinese Delegation to the League of Nations 105

China Has Gained International Sympathy

Justice Will Eventually Prevail After a Long Time

The Continental Daily reported that Dr. Li Weishi, an American advisor to the Chinese delegation to the League of Nations in Geneva, arrived in Shanghai on the President Jefferson on Tuesday night. A reporter specially visited him to inquire about the situation in Geneva. He said that Yan Huiqing, Gu Weijun, Guo Taiqi, and other representatives of China displayed their talents on the diplomatic stage, and finally made the League of Nations General Assembly publish a judgment condemning the Japanese aggression, which is worthy of pride. The three representatives presented facts and analyzed legal principles in Geneva, which were precise and touched on the key points, and were able to gain the trust of politicians and diplomats from the forty countries attending the League of Nations General Assembly. After careful investigation and thorough discussion, they finally recognized that the statements made by the Chinese representatives were true. This judgment, which maintained China's sovereignty in Manchuria, can be regarded as a great spiritual victory for China. Therefore, China now occupies a leading position in the world, and at the same time, it can be regarded as the greatest achievement in international law. At the beginning, there were rumors that since the case involved a strong country, the League of Nations would deviate from justice and demean itself to please Japan. Now, after the League of Nations General Assembly adopted the report of the Committee of Nineteen, clearly designating the aggressor, all rumors have been refuted. Afterwards, the reporter raised two questions: Since the League of Nations has shown courage, maintained justice, and helped China, what will be the next step? Will it impose sanctions to punish the Japanese? Mr. Li did not answer directly, but asked the reporter, "Why has Japan's heavy industry been working day and night since last summer?" He also said that China has obtained one of the world's strongest social essences, which cannot be used to expect immediate gains, but can win the final victory. He firmly believes that justice will eventually prevail after a long time. Mr. Li also said that he is currently compiling the final report to be submitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and will go to Beijing as soon as it is completed. According to reports, Mr. Li served as Gu Weijun's advisor when the League of Nations investigation team came to the East to investigate last year, and accompanied him to Manchuria, knowing the truth about the Manchurian case. He then went to Geneva in November to serve as an advisor to the Chinese delegation. At the beginning of this year, he went to the United States from Geneva due to important tasks, and is now coming to Shanghai from the United States.

Yoshizawa Scheduled to Go North 106

The Great American Evening News reported that Yoshizawa Kenkichi, the former Japanese Foreign Minister, announced today (the 6th) that he will leave Shanghai for the north on the Dalian Steamship Company's Changchun Maru on Saturday. After staying in Qingdao for a while, he will go to Manchuria. Viscount Iwakura and Congressman Hashizume, who are traveling with him, will visit Hangzhou this morning and return to Shanghai tomorrow night, leaving for the north together on Saturday.

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Cables the National Chamber of Commerce to Raise Funds to Save the Country 107

Designated Bank Custody

Strictly Regulate Usage

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed all chambers of commerce and overseas Chinese chambers of commerce yesterday, stating that the chamber is concerned that foreign troubles are becoming increasingly urgent, and the loss of territory is expanding daily. It is necessary to quickly plan to enrich the air force, assist the righteous men in the Northeast, restrain the Beijing area, make the Japanese enemies exhausted, and prepare military supplies for the anti-Japanese soldiers in North China to increase their combat power. Otherwise, the disaster of aggression will spread to the whole country and cause an unmanageable situation. Therefore, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Aviation Save-the-Nation Donation Custody Committee and the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Fundraising and Rescue Northeast Donation Office are established to concentrate the strength of the business community and jointly seek to resist insults. Aviation donations and rescue Northeast donations are designated to be stored and managed by reliable banks and money shops. In the future, if there is no need to purchase aircraft, the aviation donations will be refunded in full to show good faith. The donations to rescue the Northeast will also be strictly regulated and limited to necessary uses, and appropriate arrangements will be made. In short, the money obtained through hard work must be used for the actual purpose of saving the country and resisting insults, and not a penny will be wasted to live up to the people of the country. This should be a firm statement to the donors. Foreign troubles are pressing, and it is urgent. Collecting more money is to enrich the effect of resisting insults by one point. I hope that you gentlemen will quickly plan for it. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce bows and asks for contributions.

Wu Zhihao Hosted a Banquet for Zhu and Xiao Last Night 108

Representative Xiao and General Zhu Gave Passionate Reports

More Than 13,000 Yuan Was Raised on the Spot

Mr. Wu Zhihao, the general manager of the Shanghai National Goods Company, hosted a banquet last night at Gongdelin for General Zhu Ziqiao and Mr. Xiao Xiange, the representative of Commander Song. Attendees included Xu Shiying, Chu Huiseng, Guo Yonglan, Wen Lanting, Yu Zuoting, Jin Runxiang, Xue Dubi, Chen Songyuan, Wu Yaqin, Shao Daren, Zhu Meixuan, Hu Xiyuan, Wu Wenjing, Ren Jinping, Zhang Zilian, Ha Shaofu, Yin Jie Fu, Tang Zihua, Sun Zhongping, Hong Shao Chen, Xue Chunsheng, Tao Leqin, and more than a hundred others. During the banquet, Mr. Wu Zhihao, General Zhu, and Representative Xiao gave heartfelt speeches and raised 13,360 yuan in national currency and 150 sets of woolen pants on the spot to aid the Northeast refugees and the volunteer army. The speeches are recorded as follows:

Wu Zhihao said that the significance of hosting a banquet for General Zhu, Representative Xiao, and all of you gentlemen today is twofold. First, from the perspective of the people, to express our gratitude to General Zhu for his meritorious service in traveling around the country and working hard for the country, and to admire the soldiers of Commander Song Zheyuan, represented by Mr. Xiao, who repelled the enemy army with big swords at Xifengkou last month, and whose spirit of sacrifice is especially admirable. Second, there are many wounded soldiers on the front lines, and the refugees are crowded together, and all supplies are lacking. We, the people in the rear, should try to provide assistance so that the frontline soldiers can make persistent efforts and resist to the end. All my colleagues who are willing to donate money for assistance can take it to the north with General Zhu before he leaves Shanghai, or General Zhu can choose to purchase urgently needed items and transport them to the front.

Representative Xiao reported on the glorious battle of the 29th Army at Xifengkou, saying that before our army responded, the enemy army had already attacked the important mountainous areas around Xifengkou, occupying high ground and using the cover of artillery and tanks to bombard and rush at our positions. The situation was fierce and dangerous. Our 29th Route Army, with its incomplete guns and equipment, felt that it would be difficult to cope with. At this time, Commander Song gathered all the generals and soldiers and gave a speech, saying, "Japan's strength was created by 20,000 brave men sacrificing in hand-to-hand combat in the Russo-Japanese War. If our 40,000 brothers are willing to sacrifice their blood, we can turn China from weak to strong. Moreover, we were fortunate not to die in the civil war. Today, we die for the country, and our descendants will be citizens of a strong country." When the whole army heard this, they were all righteous and eager to be in the vanguard. The eight-character military order of "Advance Without Retreat, Death is the End" was issued on the spot, and the entire big sword team was led by Brigade Commander Zhao, who accepted the order despite his injuries and set off on a detour around Tie Menguan and somewhere else. In the dark night, they hurried and rushed past the enemy's front line, reaching the heavy artillery team's position, using the fire in the four fields as a signal, and advancing on three sides at the same time, using broadswords to attack and kill. After repeated victories, the Japanese enemies encountered this strong enemy and were at a loss. Therefore, they did not expect that in an instant, the sound of killing shook the sky, blood flowed into rivers, and corpses lay all over the field. The Japanese invaders all knelt down and begged for forgiveness, abandoned their weapons and fled. In this battle, after three days and nights of fierce fighting, a total of 18 heavy artillery pieces were captured, countless guns and ammunition, a military flag personally awarded by the Japanese Emperor, and many tanks were destroyed. The enemy suffered 10,000 deaths, and our side suffered about 4,000 casualties. At this point, the Xifengkou area was completely recaptured by our army. However, there were a large number of wounded soldiers, as many as five or six days. The rear hospitals were extremely lacking, and there were no cars to transport them, resulting in many injured soldiers dying halfway due to the long distance and the fact they were carried. This is a painful thing for us, and a regrettable loss. Now I hear that the people in the rear are doing their best to help set up hospitals and provide all kinds of military supplies.

General Zhu reported on the work done over the past eight months: 1. The people of the Northeast, after being under the control of the violent Japanese, have not succumbed to the violent enemy. On one occasion, more than 2,000 villagers in Pingjinshan hated the Japanese to the bone. They were driven to the top of the mountain and shot to death with machine guns. Only one child was left, who was still seriously injured. This inhuman act is truly outrageous. 2. The enemy is very short of food and often forces the people to exchange food for an unlimited number of counterfeit national banknotes, and uses the counterfeit banknotes to pay the troops of the puppet state. Their intention is to rob our food and drive our ignorant people with worthless counterfeit banknotes. The viciousness of their means is imaginable. 3. Recently, our army seized a map of Manchuria from the enemy. On it, the borders of Inner Mongolia and Manchuria are all marked with very thick national border lines. Only the provinces of Hebei and other provinces bordering our Great Wall are not marked with lines or analyzed by boundary. It is then the intention of the Japanese side is not limited to occupying Rehe and the Great Wall area, but to further take our Hebei and Shandong provinces, or even attempt to change the color of our map to fulfill their dream of annexation. The people of the country can be awakened. 4. Whenever a wounded soldier is carried to the hospital, because they have been fighting in the sandy field for a long time, their clothes, pants, and socks are all soaked in hot blood and mud, drying and wetting again and again countless times. Therefore, once injured, the clothes they are wearing are firmly attached to their skin and flesh. If you want to treat their injuries, you must use iron scissors to cut open their clothes, so the pain they suffer is another layer of pain.

Finally, those present generously pledged to donate 13,360 yuan and 150 sets of woolen shirts and pants, which were handed over to General Zhu to transport north for temporary use. It is estimated that the Textile Industry Association contributed 5,000 yuan, Yu Zuoting, Zhu Meixuan, Jin Runxiang, Xue Chunsheng, Wu Yaqin, Hu Xiyuan, and Ren Jinping contributed 5,000 yuan, Wen Lanting contributed 1,000 yuan, which is temporarily designated to subsidize the wounded soldiers' hospital organized by the Guanghua Temple Charity Group in Beiping. The Cotton Cloth Industry Association contributed 1,000 yuan, Zhang Zilian contributed 500 yuan, and medicine worth 500-600 yuan. The Crepe Industry Association contributed 500 yuan, Shao Daren donated 150 sets of woolen shirts and pants, Guo Yonglan donated 300 yuan, and Wu Wenjing donated 200 yuan.

The Northeastern Righteous People Beg for Help 109

Yang Zhibin and Others Telegraphed the Story of Killing the Enemy

Hiding in the Wilderness, Asking for Assistance to Reorganize and Try Again

The Northeast Volunteer Army Relief Association in this city received a telegram yesterday from Yang Zhibin and other righteous people from the Northeast, saying, "Since the Japanese invaders occupied the Northeast, seventeen months have passed in a blink of an eye. In these seventeen months, the Japanese invaders have used their gradual encroachment and devouring plans every day to achieve their goals, occupying our land, massacring our people, and arousing the common hatred of all people and the common anger of heaven and man. Anyone with blood and energy cannot help but be furious. Zhibin, Yongzi, and others, motivated by the sense of duty of the common people, gathered righteous men and raised their arms to kill the enemy. The anti-Japanese experience is briefly described below, as a cry to the people of the country. Zhibin, Yongzi, and Zhao Zaiyin had more than 30,000 men. In May and June of last year, they attacked Fangzheng County, defeating the rebel army of Yu Shencheng, Li Wenbing, and Liu Yushu in Tongzigou, and defeating the Japanese army at Hongtuya, killing more than 200 Japanese soldiers, and sinking two Japanese warships in the Songhua River. In July and August, they captured Hecheng, and the rebel army of Chen Decai was defeated and scattered, killing more than 300 Japanese soldiers. In September and October, they attacked Shuangcheng and fought bloodily for three nights, finally recapturing it, and incorporating the 1,500 men of the rebel army of Zhang Yingjie, killing more than 50 Japanese soldiers. In November, they sent a team to blow up the Songhua River Bridge on the Ha-Chang Line, and more than 20 Japanese military vehicles fell into the water, and the Ha-Chang Road was blocked for more than ten days. This is a brief overview of the anti-Japanese efforts of Zhibin, Yongzi, and others. (omitted) The comrades are exposed to the wind and rain, sleep in the snow and eat frost, break through the forest of guns and brave the rain of bullets, and hide in the wilderness. For four days, they do not know the taste of salt. The various predicaments are too numerous to describe. Alas, to prevent Baishan from collapsing, we must throw our heads. To seek the long flow of the Blackwater, we must pour out iron blood. Han Guang and others have promised their bodies to the country and have no regard for anything else. As long as there is a breath left, we will definitely fight the Japanese invaders to the end. We only hope that the people of the country will give us assistance and generously contribute to the righteous cause. One bullet can kill one enemy, and one dou of millet can feed one soldier. We must enable patriotic men to continue their work, and the recovery of lost territories can be expected. Weeping and stating our case, we implore you to understand. Song Yongzi, Zhao Zaiyin, Wang Hanguang, Hou Laozhen, Wang Caichen, Liu Guodong, Yang Zhibin, and Rui Daoyi, Righteous People of the Northeast.

The International Trade Bureau Plans to Formulate State-Run Measures for Sino-Russian Trade 111

Currently Under Study by Various Departments of the Ministry of Industry

Formal Consultations Will Be Held After the Russian Envoy Arrives in Shanghai

The Sino-Russian trade issue, since the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, the Ministry of Industry has been striving for state-run operation to avoid creating one-sided dumping. According to news from the International Trade Bureau, regarding the Sino-Russian trade issue, the two sides have exchanged views informally. Our side absolutely advocates state-run operation, while the Russian side opposes this move. Moreover, the Russian economy relies on exports for its maintenance, so it has made demands for trade between the two sides. The payment for goods exported to Russia cannot be made in cash, while the payment for goods exported to China must be made in cash, resulting in a large difference between the two sides. At the same time, the International Trade Bureau has reported from tea merchants that the export of Chinese tea to Russia has always required payment within fifteen months, causing tea merchants to be limited by their financial resources and unable to operate. And upon investigation, the major exports from our country to Russia are only tea and soybeans. After the loss of the three northeastern provinces, its position has been lost. Due to the above situation, tea in the Russian market has been completely taken over by Japanese tea and Ceylon tea. Therefore, according to this situation, we are only a market for others, forming one-sided dumping. Although Sino-Russian relations have now restored friendly relations, it is necessary to have state-run operation to maintain our country's industry and commerce, and to regulate equality. Therefore, the principle of state-run operation has been decided by the Central Political Conference, and the measures have also been submitted by the International Trade Bureau for adoption by the Ministry of Industry. The most important points include two: (1) The principle of exports is not to hinder our raw materials and people's food needs. (2) The principle of imports is not to hinder our inherent industries and small industries. And there are three ways: (1) Organize the Sino-Russian Trade Company to specialize in its affairs. (2) Organize a banking group by various banks to handle the exchange of funds for import and export goods. (3) The National Bank assists in this matter. These measures are currently under study by the various departments of the Ministry of Industry, and formal consultations will be held after the Russian envoy arrives in Shanghai.

Amidst anxiety and indignation, he coughed up a lot of blood yesterday morning

Doctor diagnoses rupture of a cardiac aortic aneurysm

Mr. Liang Shiyi previously came to Shanghai from Hong Kong, intending to go north to participate in the anti-Japanese war effort. His family members have already rushed to his side separately.

This amendment adds "those who own or operate factories or engage in industry" to the list of those required to obtain a license.

If there are any errors or omissions, they must notify the Revenue Office for correction by April 13th. Blank forms for this authorization can be obtained from the Revenue Office and must be submitted by 4:00 PM on the 18th at the latest. The proposals for this special meeting are of great importance, and the Municipal Council hopes that taxpayers will responsibly attend and participate in the discussions.

Ineffective Prohibition of Prostitution in the Concession 115

League of Nations Review of the Report on the Investigation of Trafficking in Women and Children

My Representative Hu Shize Points Out Various Errors

Geneva, 5th (Havas) – The League of Nations Advisory Committee on the Protection of Children and Youth continued to review the report of the Far East Investigation Mission on Trafficking in Women and Children and listened to the explanation of Chinese Representative Hu Shize. Mr. Hu praised the investigation mission for overcoming various difficulties and finally completing its work, but said that the narrative part of the report gave the world the impression that Chinese women were most likely to fall into brothels, which was inevitably wrong. Regarding various proposals to prevent trafficking in women, Mr. Hu said that China agreed to establish a supervisory body under the central government, and that closer cooperation among local authorities in various places was especially necessary. This was because the situation in some parts of China was unique. For example, in Shanghai alone, the municipal government prohibited the opening of brothels, while the concession allowed them, which was one aspect of it. Regarding the fact that most of the staff in institutions protecting women and children were women, Mr. Hu stated that since the Chinese revolution, women could also seek employment, no different from men. As for the special issue of Russian women, Mr. Hu said that most of these women came from Manchuria, and the Chinese government could not bear responsibility for this part of the territory. Furthermore, Russian women who became prostitutes mostly did so within the concession. Finally, Mr. Hu repeatedly stated that the report acknowledged that the Chinese government was making great efforts to prohibit prostitution and hoped that education could prevent the scourge of brothels in the future, so that they would not spread.
