Japanese Division Commander Conference, Army Minister Araki Barks Madly 232

Using the Guise of an Extraordinary Period to Encourage Militarism Among the People

Supplementing Military Personnel and Preventing Communist Infiltration

China United News Agency, Tokyo: The highly anticipated Japanese National Division Commander Conference opened at 9:00 AM on the 30th of last month in the First Conference Room of the Ministry of the Army. In an atmosphere of extreme tension, Army Minister Araki gave a lengthy speech, the content of which is worthy of attention. The outline is as follows:

Understanding of the Current Situation: The importance of the current domestic and international situation was explained in great detail at the team leader conference convened last spring and at the end of last year. There is no need to repeat it here. Since Japan officially recognized "Manchukuo" on September 15th of last year and resolutely withdrew from the League of Nations recently, the Japanese Empire has been in a state of external isolation and internal chaos. However, our soldiers have been able to overcome difficulties and deal with the crisis in this extraordinary period, which is a cause for celebration for the future of the Empire. I hope that everyone will be even more determined to fulfill the mission of defending the country, prepare for total national mobilization, and properly handle even greater crises in the future.

Leadership and Guidance of the Army: Since we soldiers have shouldered such a major mission, in order to give full play to the essence of the army, we must strengthen the consolidation of leadership within the army and the strict guidance of organizational activities and the spirit of control. The central leadership is paying special attention to this point. After several studies, it is believed that it is necessary to give special respect and support to the position and authority of the team leaders at all levels, who are the driving force of the organization, and especially to strictly lead and supervise the newly appointed young officers, and to guide them with love, so that the entire army can reflect on itself, unite under strict military discipline, and strive to revitalize itself.

Implementation of the Military Reform Plan: The Military Improvement Plan to save the situation, which has been planned for a long time, has been passed by the 64th National Diet. This is one of the main countermeasures of the army. As long as the budget is approved, it will be implemented immediately. The Military Reform Plan is designed to adapt to the urgency of the situation. The content of the improvement of various systems is based on the emergency projects of 1933 and 1934. However, it is believed that it can be implemented as a permanent improvement when necessary.

Supplement of Personnel: Regarding the disposition of combat personnel, a full account was given at last year's Division Commander Conference. In order to consolidate the strength of leadership, it is necessary to promote excellent technical personnel and to strengthen the combat team leaders. The central leadership is paying special attention to this point. I hope that everyone can conscientiously select new talents. Also, with the implementation of the military reform, the expansion of special volunteer officers and the increase in the number of special warrant officers should be appropriately allocated. As for the employment of special volunteer officers, special attention should be paid to their resumes and character. They should be admitted only after a thorough review. We should step up precautions against the infiltration of communist elements.

Regarding the Military Budget: In view of the current state of Japan's finances and economy, the world often holds pessimistic views. However, we firmly believe that the people can bear this huge budget. Although the national finances have continuously increased a lot of deficit bonds in this extraordinary period, it is necessary to do so in order to save the current emergency. I hope that everyone can understand the current state of the national finances and the purpose of this budget, and strive to eliminate all kinds of waste and actively use it for appropriate military improvement and the supplementation of technical personnel.

Regarding the Support of the Entire People: In modern warfare, the most important thing is the total mobilization of the entire people, who can be the shield of national defense. Therefore, we should strive to mobilize all forces, expand and strengthen the organization of national defense associations and air defense associations in various places, actively explain the internal and external crisis situation, and ensure that the entire people can eliminate the import of foreign ideas under the command of the military and move forward under the mission of saving the country.

Reorganization of the Veterans' Association: Since the beginning of the war, veterans across the country have been able to rise up to serve the country, which is truly commendable. However, at this time, the Veterans' Association should reform all the pending issues and internal structure, strive to make up for its shortcomings, strengthen the spirit of military-civilian unity, thoroughly implement national salvation education, and make it more powerful to serve national defense.

Training of Students and Youth: Pure youth and students are often confused by foreign ideas. You should provide them with special education. In particular, students in higher schools need more active guidance. The system of reserve officers will soon be revised and implemented. Therefore, the student training in higher schools across the country must be reorganized. Especially, the persons in charge of the schools should strive to revitalize it and step up the supervision and guidance of student ideology. Youth are the most important part of the country's long-term plan. Youth training centers in various places must provide them with practical assistance and education. (Omitted below)

British House of Commons Passes the Bill to Ban Russian Imports on Third Reading 233

Effective for Three Months from the Date of Publication

Foreign Secretary Hopes It Will Not Be Implemented

British Lawyers Go to Moscow to Attend the Trial

Reuters, London, 6th: The bill to ban Russian imports was passed on the third reading in the House of Commons today by a vote of 291 to 41. Liberal Party members such as Samuel voted in favor on the third reading because Trade Minister Runciman announced an amendment stipulating that the ban would only be effective for three months from the date of publication and would be repealed if not continued after the expiration. The continuation of this ban would also require the consent of Parliament. Runciman, in response to questions from former Foreign Secretary Chamberlain, Liberal Party leader Samuel, and others, said that what needs to be understood now is that the power conferred by this bill can only be exercised when the detention of British engineers reaches a serious point. Foreign Secretary Simon concluded the debate on the bill, saying that he hoped that the bill would not be implemented, but that the possibility depended on the Russian authorities.

Reuters, London, 6th: London lawyer Dunner, legal counsel for Vickers, will go to Moscow tonight to attend the trial of the arrested British engineers. The Russian authorities have now confirmed that the trial will open on April 10th. The Russian consul in London has issued a passport to Dunner, accompanied by a skilled Russian interpreter. Vickers has also authorized Mr. Monkhouse, the head of its Moscow branch, to hire lawyers to defend the engineers, who are also defendants. The Soviet Foreign Minister replied that one British lawyer could be allowed to attend the trial. London considered this unsatisfactory and is still making every effort to persuade the Soviet Union to allow the engineers to have British lawyers as consultants and assist them during the trial. Sir Paul, chairman of Vickers, said in London today that the Soviet Union had made a big mistake. He was particularly pleased that the engineers had received strict orders from the company not to get involved in the political or other disputes of the Soviet government.

Reuters, Moscow, 6th: The bailers of the five British defendants from Vickers were notified today that they could inspect the detailed text of the charges tomorrow to prepare a defense. It is said that the defendants do not want to rely on the lawyers provided by the court and will hire lawyers from the members of the Bar Association.

Japanese Intellectual Class Unemployed, No Relief Available 235

According to the Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun, the number of unemployed intellectuals in Tokyo Prefecture and Tokyo City is increasing daily. For emergency relief, last year there were 1,307,642 unemployed people, and the relief fund was 1,406,000 yen. This year, the number has increased to 1,527,700 yen, with the number of people reaching 1,176,500. The number of people who are relieved and employed daily is only 3,515, less than one-tenth of the unemployed. The actual number of unemployed is likely to be several times higher. Moreover, the number of new graduates from schools is increasing year by year, while the employment by government offices and city governments is very small. Many private companies are unable to provide appropriate placement. Therefore, from the 7th to the 8th year of the Showa era, the number reached 138,800, an average increase of approximately 2,381 people per day. According to actual estimates, the number of unemployed should increase by 3,185 people. Since the year before last, the number of unemployed has been increasing year by year. On September 1, Showa 6, it was 25,462; in December of the same year, it was 32,559; and in January of the 8th year, it was 35,744. The Tokyo City government has planned relief measures for the unemployed and set conditions, stipulating that for university graduates, the daily allowance is 1.5 yen during a certain probationary period; for vocational school graduates, it is 1.2 yen per day; and for secondary school graduates, it is 0.9 yen per day. Half of the salary burden is subsidized by the national treasury, and the other half is borne by the employing organization. However, private organizations are still not enthusiastic about the trial employment idea. Therefore, the number of unemployed from January 1st of this year to the present has reached 96,300. However, recently, due to the impact of the current situation, it has been easier for skilled workers to find employment in military factories. As for other unemployed people, there are no relief measures available.

Factory Inspection Implemented in Concessions

Factory Inspection 240

However, regarding the method, they require us to send trained inspection personnel to be under the control of the concession authorities. However, the Factory Law was promulgated by the National Government, and the Municipal Government is ordered to implement it. This kind of request actually hinders our administrative power. Moreover, the citizens of the concession should naturally abide by the orders of the Chinese government and be protected by the Chinese government. Therefore, the administrative power of the Chinese government can naturally be implemented in the concession, so that the Chinese and foreign boundaries are treated equally. Because of this, there has not been a substantial result. However, the Yangjingbang Regulations also clearly stipulate that the amendment of the articles must also be approved by the Chinese government before it can take effect.

Police System 241

Tax Collection 242

The business tax is suspended. The preparation for the collection of land value tax has been fully completed. Reconstruction Situation 243

Since the allocation of funds for the plan to revitalize the prosperity of the city, it has been actively implemented. The construction of main roads and municipal libraries and hospitals has been implemented in order. The progress is quite rapid. The municipal government building and various main roads in the city center area will also be completed separately. However, the entire project will have to be completed by the end of this year. Therefore, although the relocation of various agencies of the municipal government was previously expected to be realized in mid-July, judging from the actual situation, it will also be at the end of this year.

Abolishing Taels and Changing to Yuan, Shanghai Merchants Comply with Convenience 246

Silver and Money Industry to Start Registering Forward Silver Notes Today

After the Ministry of Finance ordered the implementation of abolishing taels and changing to yuan, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has today announced to all industries to comply. The silver and money industry feels quite convenient. The Banking Association has started to register forward silver notes. The details are recorded as follows:

Chamber of Commerce Announcement 247

Now, we have received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance, stating that the Ministry has now decided that from April 6th, all receipts and payments of public and private funds, as well as the signing of contracts, notes, and all transactions, must be uniformly changed to silver coins, and silver taels must no longer be used. For those that were originally stipulated to be received and paid in silver taels before this date, the standard in Shanghai should be to convert one silver tael of treasury yuan into one silver coin. The receipts and payments should be made in silver coins. In other places outside Shanghai, the treasury yuan should first be converted according to the Shanghai exchange rate on April 5th, and then the treasury yuan should be converted into silver coins. After this date, new contracts and notes, and the receipts and payments of public and private funds, and all transactions that still use silver taels, will be legally invalid. Those who hold silver taels may, in accordance with the regulations for the minting of silver standard coins, request the Central Mint to mint silver coins on their behalf, or send them to the local Central Bank of China and Bank of Communications to exchange for silver coins for circulation, in order to facilitate matters. In addition to posting this notice and distributing it to various industries, we have urgently telegraphed to inform you and request that you forward it to your subordinates for compliance. This notice.

[P Suitable for Both Chinese and Foreign>

A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency met a leader of the silver and money industry this morning. According to him, after the Ministry of Finance's order to abolish taels arrived in Shanghai, member meetings were convened separately to decide on domestic and foreign measures. All incoming and outgoing silver tael funds were converted into silver yuan for transfer yesterday according to the rate of 715. The issuance of silver notes has been suspended. This matter happened suddenly, and foreign merchant banks initially found it difficult to receive and deliver. Now, foreign merchant banks have decided to convert the receipt and delivery of silver taels from Chinese merchants into silver yuan. Therefore, there is no difficulty at all, and it is actually more convenient. As for the conversion rate of 715, it is the legal price set by the government, and all industries abide by it uniformly, so there are no problems with silver tael transfers.

Registration 248

The Silver and Money Industry Association has decided to submit eight resolutions of the member meeting to the Ministry of Finance this afternoon for transfer to the judicial authorities for record. As for the forward silver tael notes that are due after April 15th, the Banking Association has decided to start registration tomorrow morning. After these notes are registered, the association will stamp a seal on the back of the note.

Increasing Unemployment Among Overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia 249

Reaching Over 284,000 People

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Formulating Relief Plan

In recent years, due to the impact of the appreciation of gold and the depreciation of silver, all businesses in various parts of Southeast Asia have shown extreme decline, especially the rubber and tin rice industries, resulting in our overseas Chinese residing in various parts of Southeast Asia being forced into unemployment. According to a survey by a reporter from the East China News Agency at the International Trade Bureau, in the past year, the total number of unemployed overseas Chinese who have returned to China from various British and Dutch possessions in Southeast Asia has reached 283,890, accounting for approximately three-tenths of the total number of overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia. Moreover, most of them are self-employed businessmen, and their total capital is no more than 1,000 yuan. Due to years of business failures, their funds have been almost completely lost. Moreover, the governments of various places in British and Dutch Southeast Asia are heavily taxing various rates. If the overseas Chinese are unable to pay, they are expelled and returned to China, resulting in unemployment. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce is now planning to investigate the unemployment of laborers, distributing forms for investigation to its subordinates. In addition, the Overseas Chinese Affairs Management Office is drafting a plan to relieve the unemployment of overseas Chinese and to encourage overseas Chinese to return to China to start businesses, and is submitting it to the Central Government for review and implementation. It is also ordering the Immigration Section to follow the precedent of immigration in various countries, collecting reference materials, and drafting an immigration law to meet the needs.

Shanghai-Hangzhou Bus Overturns 253

The Accident Site is Near Xiaotang

More Than Ten Passengers in the Car Injured

At 12:40 PM yesterday, a tragic accident occurred near Xiaotang on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway when a Shanghai-Hangzhou public bus overturned. More than ten passengers in the car were injured. The details obtained by a reporter from the East China News Agency are recorded below:

Cause of the Accident 254

Since the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway opened to traffic on October 10th last year, it has been very convenient for transportation. However, accidents have occurred from time to time. At 2:40 PM yesterday afternoon, a Shanghai-Hangzhou public bus picked up more than ten passengers in Minhang. While being driven by Zhu Liang, the bus had only traveled a few miles when, near Xiaotang, in an attempt to avoid a child, the driver steered the car into a ditch on the side of the road. He was unable to brake in time, causing the bus to overturn. The passengers in the car were all thrown about, suffering severe shocks, injuries, and bleeding. The windows of the bus were also shattered. After the accident, the villagers came forward to help the passengers out of the bus one by one.

Fortunately, No Deaths 255

However, all the passengers had bleeding limbs and back pain to varying degrees. The slightly injured passengers were not far from their homes, so they all walked home. Those who were more seriously injured were helped across the river by the villagers and sent to Minhang Hospital for treatment.

Injury Investigation 256

This morning, a reporter from the East China News Agency drove to the accident site to investigate. The wrecked bus had already been repaired in Minhang. The body of the car was slightly damaged, and several pieces of glass were shattered. The damage is estimated to be around one or two hundred yuan. He also visited Mr. Huang Bingjun, the director of Minhang Hospital, to inquire about the condition of the injured. According to him, after the injured passengers arrived at the hospital, they were all slightly injured. After being bandaged, they were discharged from the hospital. Therefore, no one stayed in the hospital last night. The injured who arrived at the hospital were Zhou Moqing, Song Yunsheng, Liang Yungeng, Wang, and Shi Xiaoqin. Among them, Wang was more seriously injured.

Robbers Shot and Killed Police Officer 257

Wu Junxuan Died in the Line of Duty

Injured Gang Member Captured

At around 5:00 AM today, just as dawn was breaking, a robbery occurred at the Jian Dao Bridge on Huining Road in Nanshi. The robbers opened fire, killing a police officer. A stray bullet accidentally injured a fellow gang member. The details are recorded on the left. Wu Junxuan, a 28-year-old Tianjin native, is a police officer at the Manufacturing Bureau Road Police Station in the Second District. He had only been on duty for six days. This morning, he was assigned to patrol the Jian Dao Bridge on Huining Road. At dawn, he saw three suspicious-looking individuals walking from east to west, talking as they walked, looking fierce and menacing. Knowing that they were not good people, he ordered them to stop. Just as he was about to step forward to search them, the robbers, knowing that they were guilty, preemptively struck. Two of the robbers rushed up and grabbed the police officer Wu's arms. The police officer immediately lost his ability to resist and could not escape. Another robber took out a pistol and shot at him, firing five shots in a row. Two shots hit him, with the bullets entering from the upper ends of his breasts on the left and right sides and exiting from his back, injuring his lungs. He immediately fell to the ground and died. A stray bullet injured a gang member named Jia (said to be from Yancheng). The robbers fled in a panic. The police officer on the next post heard the gunshots and rushed over to investigate. Seeing Jia running wildly, he knew what they had done and chased after him. He chased him all the way to Sanguantang, where he finally captured Jia. The rest escaped. Jia was escorted to the Second District Police Station, where it was found that he was seriously injured. He was immediately sent to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. Police were dispatched to the scene of the incident to collect five bullet casings from the ground. At the same time, the local land officials were ordered to report to the local court for an autopsy. Later, the prosecutor arrived at the scene and confirmed that the police officer Wu Junxuan had indeed died from gunshot wounds. He filled out a form ordering that the body be collected and prepared for instructions. It was found that the police officer's hometown had an elderly mother, a wife, and a five-year-old son, all of whom depended on the police officer for their livelihood.

Arawazawa is Coming! 259

— Me

In recent days, the spring scenery has become brighter day by day, and the situation outside the pass is becoming more peaceful day by day. Why is Arawazawa coming to China? Everyone knows that the reason is sufficient. It is not just for sightseeing, but also to visit "old friends." Now, there is another resolute non-reception to show determination, which is really enough to tell the gods and demons and illuminate the sun and moon. Transcendental Occupation 260

— Jingxian

I am unemployed, but I am not a vagrant.

The kind of work I do doesn't require much capital at all, and it's not included in the three hundred and sixty professions. Talking about investing capital to make profits, or making a huge profit from a small investment, it all looks like robbery to me. Snatching other people's money, swindling other people's money, desperately stuffing it into one's own pocket, that's shameful.

Some people say, if you don't spend much capital, are you a master of begging?

Bah, I wouldn't even look at that. I wouldn't secretly become a bastard pickpocket either.

If a person has two hands like nail rakes, why worry about food and drink? I've also had thousands upon thousands of colorful bills in my pockets, and I've even had a courtesan as a concubine. What haven't I done? Little ones, jumping and jumping with all their energy, trembling and trembling, bah, what's so rare about that? If I hadn't watched thousands upon thousands of silver dollars slip through my fingers, who would dare to look down on me today?

Well, I've seen through everything now. Wealth and glory are nothing but that. Spending the whole day bragging and boasting, sticking out your stiff leg, you can't take it into the coffin, so what's the point?

I am unemployed, but I am not a vagrant.

My life is somewhat like those little guys who go to the theater and hang out with women. I don't feel any energy until I go out at three or four in the afternoon.

Every day at three or four in the afternoon, I take a bamboo stick about two feet long, carry two yellow pockets, and walk along the road like an old woman going on a pilgrimage, bowing all the way. No, damn it, what bodhisattvas, what lords, pretending to deceive people, even though I'm poor to the bone, I won't even give them a second glance. I am looking for cigarette butts on the road.

I look for cigarette butts on the road, only filling twelve pockets a day. When two pockets are full, I take them to that fellow Zhang Si's shop. That fellow Zhang Si is really a good friend. Two pockets of cigarette butts, no more, no less, regardless of quality, he always gives me half a string of cash. Eight coppers, I exchange for a meal and a drink. Eight coppers, I save for tomorrow's food and drink. As for the extra, haha, speaking of which, I perk up. Red pills, I don't like to smoke. You're welcome. Opium paste is enough for me to enjoy day and night.

I don't like to look for them at the tram station. Those skinflints who ride the tram like to puff on cigarettes until their lips are swollen before they throw away the cigarette butts. If they don't do that, they won't be able to sleep all night. It's even less use looking in front of the bank. Those who go in and out of that bank, each one has to be weighed on a scale to see how heavy they are, and they are even more hopeless than me. Never in their lives will a cigarette butt as thick as the sky fall from their dog mouths.

Movie theaters, theaters, San Dong Yi Pin, No. 181, in front of these places, there's gold all over the ground, as long as your two nail rakes are willing to move. The little guys in their nice Western suits look like devils from behind, holding women with big butts, jumping and jumping, trembling and trembling, going in and out, as if they can't take their cigarettes inside, so they throw them away at the door. I pick them up with my big bamboo chopsticks, damn it, at least an inch long. White tin foil is the minimum, and there are plenty that I don't even know the names of. Mei Li Brand, White Gold Dragon, bah, Chinese goods. Picking up Chinese cigarette butts is hopeless. I don't like to smoke Chinese cigarettes.

I am unemployed, but I am not a vagrant. I don't become an official, I don't do business, I don't steal, I don't rob, I don't swindle, I don't beg. I do something that doesn't deceive heaven and earth, doesn't deceive my ancestors, and is not included in the three hundred and sixty professions. White rice, brown rice, no need to worry, damn it, it's more comfortable than anything else.

That young fellow Wang Xiaoliuzi went to Huangpu to jump in the river the day before yesterday, what a fool. He was born with a pair of nail rakes, how could he not find food and drink? Half a string a day, without spending a penny, it's all mine, haha.

Page 18

April Fool's Day 261

— Xi

April 1st is the Westerners' "April Fool's Day." According to Western customs, on this day each year, one can "tell lies" and "fool" friends without being considered "insulting." However, the origin of this matter is unverifiable.

Some say: Westerners "lie" and are allowed to "tell" lies, and even specially set up a "holiday" for it, which is tantamount to promoting a cunning style. If this style persists, with mutual deception and mutual fooling, can the morality and people's hearts still be inquired about? Our noble country still hangs the golden signboard of "Land of Propriety and Righteousness" and "Integrity as the Foundation." Therefore, there used to be as many as twenty-four solar terms, and now, due to the eastward spread of European customs, we have added "Women's Day," "Children's Day," "Teachers' Day," "Labor Day," "Anti-Smoking Day," and so on. However, we do not popularize the April Fool's Day, and even the highly Westernized Chinese rarely inquire about it, fearing that it conflicts with the golden signboard, and there is a difficult dilemma of "difficult to comply with."

It is not known that although our noble country does not have an officially determined and promulgated April Fool's Day in name, in reality, the generally clever countrymen, especially the generals who are responsible for defending the territory, have long been "taking the lead" in popularizing "lying." It's just that they have not formally "chosen an auspicious day to open" and clearly stipulated which day is the holiday.

Before the loss of Rehe, they telegraphed the whole country, expressing "determination to resist" and issuing statements, expressing "vowing to defend the territory to the death." When it was lost, they said, "This was expected" and "It is not difficult to counterattack"!

The Southwest authorities, regarding the military expedition to resist Japan, I heard that they have already decided on a specific plan and have conducted a swearing-in ceremony. However, the words "going north immediately" are like the wonderful use of "long-term resistance," not afraid of wearing through as many as 470 million pairs of eyes!

"Punishing the puppet state," "recovering lost territory," "counterattacking Chengde," have oiled the mouths of important people and made the ears of the people of the country tired, almost completely becoming a modern myth of the great Republic of China in the 20th century that has oiled mouths and tired ears!

Recently, Mr. XX is also singing loudly: "Before the end of this year, the lost territory in the Northeast can definitely be restored." A certain member of the Central Committee also predicted that "Japan will definitely have a major revolution within ten years." The affirmative tone seems to be more accurate than Yuan Tiangang's Tui Bei Tu and Liu Bowen's Shao Bing Ge.

In other cases, the Supervisory Yuan once impeached a certain official, but what was the result of the conviction? It is often like a stone sinking into the sea. Shops falsely claim to be selling domestic goods, but in reality, they are selling enemy goods; hanging up signs for quitting smoking medicine, but actually selling opium; boasting greatly about sacrificing capital, but adding a large promotional fee to the price of goods. Everything, everything, is to the best of our ability to "lie" and gather the great achievements of "fooling" compatriots. For 360 days a year, almost every day, many people are "lying" and "fooling" compatriots, which is no different from celebrating the Eastern-style "April Fool's Day" every day!

But keep in mind: Westerners only have April 1st, keeping in mind the warning of being fooled. Our country has to listen to the nonsense of "just speaking casually" all year round, and it is impossible to guard against it. This is obviously because we have been fooled. I don't know if we should imitate the Westerners and regard it as a great insult, which has led to the other party's "deep-rooted" bad habits!

Clerks' Correspondence

The True Meaning of Marriage 262

Editor:

I am a weak woman of seventeen—not a clerk—I don't think you will reject my request, right? My father unfortunately passed away last year, and now there is only a loving mother and a weak younger brother at home. When I was twelve years old, my father arranged a marriage for me. At that time, I didn't understand anything, and everything was decided by my parents. The other party is now twenty-five years old and works as a partner in a shop. Although his monthly income is small, he knows how to be frugal. His appearance is ordinary, but his temperament is mild. All of this was told to me by my mother. In my heart, I am somewhat unwilling to marry. There are three reasons for my unwillingness: (1) the age difference is eight years, (2) the other party's family has no permanent property, (3) the wedding is scheduled for the end of this year, so I want to cancel the engagement, but there are also three difficulties: (1) my mother is quite in favor of it. If I resolutely oppose it, it will definitely make my mother unhappy, and I will also be uneasy, (2) photos and birth dates have been exchanged during the engagement, and there is a matchmaker as a witness, (3) after canceling the engagement, whether choosing another match can be more satisfactory than the previous one, I am not sure! I have no decisiveness—I rely entirely on you, sir—to give me a satisfactory answer in the newspaper.

Sincerely, Luo Yuping, a weak woman, April 3rd

乂　　乂　　乂　　乂　　乂

Editor's note: Blind marriages are now criticized by the general public. If Ms. Luo has realized that the other party has aspects that are "unworthy of being a partner," then she may as well raise the issue of canceling the engagement. The law also provides considerable protection because this has not been done with the consent of the person. However, judging from Ms. Luo's letter, although her father arranged the engagement for her five years ago, she has not even met the other party. Therefore, although Ms. Luo raises three reasons for her unwillingness, we believe that they are all superficial unwillingness and not unwillingness based on genuine understanding. Let's first study these three reasons:

Regarding the first point, in ancient times, "men marry at thirty and women marry at twenty"; according to physiology, the couple should also follow the principle that the woman is younger than the man, and the woman's appearance is easier to age than the man's. Therefore, we believe that the age difference is not a problem. As for the second point, we believe that we should not take "having permanent property or not having permanent property" as the standard, but should take "whether or not there is self-reliance ability" as the standard. We deeply agree with the third point. Ms. Luo may use her young age as an excuse and ask her mother to ask someone to discuss with the other party and postpone it for a year or half a year. During this year and a half, first establish a kind of friendly acquaintance (but do not let the concept of "already engaged" be preconceived), and then carefully observe the other party's temperament, ability, and other aspects. This way, it can be more real than what you hear. At that time, if you find that the other party does have aspects that are "unworthy of being a partner," then raising the issue of canceling the engagement will not make the "difficulty" a "difficulty." If you can get along well with each other, then during this year and a half of friendship, the seeds of love will grow, and the result will be a satisfactory marriage. Because the true meaning of marriage is built on "love."

Fiction

Dream Time (23rd continuation) 265

— Qin Shouou

Wu Yi had no siblings, and he regarded Miss Mao with as much joy and care as if she were his own little sister, often praising her endlessly in front of his wife, Miss Liu. Miss Liu's response each time was always a mysterious smile, but she absolutely did not restrict Wu Yi from going to the Wang family. She still quietly and patiently took care of the household affairs, unknowingly planting the seeds of Wu Yi's later epiphany.

"What? Isn't she home today?" Miss Mao loved music the most, and she was especially good at playing the piano. Wu Yi always came to Yu Lin's house at about 6:30 every day, as if he had made an appointment with her. Similarly, she would start playing her favorite Western music on the Pia Xiana from 6:15 every day until Wu Yi pushed the door in to stop her. Today, Wu Yi arrived on time as usual, but the sound of the piano was silent, making him hesitate outside the door, not daring to go in.

"The young mistress is sick! She's lying upstairs!" He finally went in, and bumped into an old nanny, who gave him a report that was actually not surprising, but which he considered to be very surprising.

He immediately felt another layer of hardship. "Lying upstairs?" Upstairs was her bedroom. Going up would inevitably seem inappropriate to onlookers, but not going up, he didn't have that decisive courage! He was like a new soldier about to go to the front line, hesitating, sometimes standing up, sometimes sitting down. No matter how careless a person was, they could definitely see his morbid state clearly.

"Uncle! Haha...!" Yu Lin's three-year-old child, Xiao Lin, suddenly came down from upstairs, hugged his Auntie Jin, and unexpectedly conveyed Miss Mao's words, saying that she was inviting Young Master Wu to come up.

Wu Yi finished a flight of twenty or thirty stairs in just two jumps.

"Sister-in-law... little friend!" He stood under a purple-red curtain, both surprised and delighted, pausing slightly, planning to formally call out "sister-in-law," but he was unwilling, and after saying one word, he stopped, still calling out softly according to the title he had predetermined in his heart. "What? Are you sick? Do you have a fever? Did you catch a cold? Yu has gone to Nanjing, why didn't you take care of yourself!"

Movie Magazine

George Raft's Inversion of All Women (Part 1) 266

— Xi Rong

One of the Most Sought-After Men by Women After the Death of Rudolph Valentino

Anyone who knows a little about the anecdotes of the film industry can remember the grand funeral of Rudolph Valentino after his death; the mourning and honor after the death of a great president could not even reach half of it. It goes without saying that Valentino was admired by women during his lifetime and was besieged by female crowds everywhere. Now, Hollywood has a second Valentino; his appearance and demeanor are almost identical to Valentino. This new star is named George Raft. Since he showed his skills in "Scarface," he has already caused a sensation among movie fans across the United States, who all say that Valentino has been resurrected. Raft was already a close friend with Valentino during his lifetime. Although one was born in Mexico and the other in New York, USA, they were able to meet in one place and work together for many years, and the two of them looked alike, and those who saw them suspected that they were brothers. It can also be said that they were a match made in heaven.

Later, Valentino gave up his dancing career and entered the film industry during his lifetime. At that time, he persuaded Raft to go to Hollywood with him, because not only could they play brothers on the screen, but also act as his double on the screen, and no one would recognize him. Unexpectedly, Raft did not want to succeed because of others, and he was unwilling to give up his dancing career, so he broke up with Valentino. Now that he has returned to Hollywood, he is separated from Valentino by the grave, and he can't help but feel a sense of vicissitudes.

Raft is also besieged by crazy women everywhere, similar to Valentino during his lifetime. Although Raft has bodyguards, secretaries, servants, etc., he still cannot prevent women from harassing Raft. Whether it is at the train station, hotel rooms, theater entrances, or around his car, they are surrounded by infatuated women: sometimes they even take advantage of people's unpreparedness and break into his bedroom, asking for a kiss; although this is said to be an endless blessing, it also makes him restless and has no freedom or fun. In addition to signing autographs and inscriptions, those who ask him for souvenirs also want to snatch his hat, handkerchief, buttonhole, buttons on his clothes, and shoelaces on his shoes. One day, Raft came out of a theater in the Tituo Lawi area and was surrounded by many women, who tore his clothes. By the time the police rescued him into the car, his upper body clothes had disappeared, and his trousers were also torn to pieces.

Valentino had a similar experience in Boston before. At that time, a group of women surrounded him at the theater entrance. By the time Valentino broke through the siege, he had almost nothing left on his body except for a few scars and blood marks. Now Raft no longer dares to walk through the main entrance of the theater, and must sneak out from the side door after the crowd has dispersed. Sometimes he sleeps in the theater room all night, and there are still naughty women who climb up the fire escape to meet him. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "The Old House Mystery" A Dangerous Affair 267

— Xing

In the past six months, "horror" films have indeed catered to the preferences of the general public and have achieved great success. Therefore, "The Old House Mystery," which was shown at the Carlton yesterday, attracted a lot of audiences.

It tells the story of a friendly patrolman and a reporter who both meet a girl. The reporter breaks into the girl's house at night to steal a necklace, intending to use it to get closer to the girl. Unexpectedly, at that time, a senior of the girl died and said in his will that all the property would be returned to the girl, but the girl must still retain the jewelry necklace she already had when accepting the inheritance. At this time, the reporter and the patrolman planned to return the necklace, but it was stolen again. So they went to the old house owned by the girl's elder to investigate, and after several twists and turns, they finally recovered the pearl. As soon as the case came to light: the reporter and the girl also fulfilled their long-cherished wish.

In the screenwriter's purpose, in addition to describing the harm of inheritance, which can make clansmen become enemies, it is only to use the color of terror to call. The meaning of the play is very shallow.

The whole film is performed entirely in a comedic way. Therefore, its horror can only be regarded as a part of the insertion. However, it cannot be regarded as a comedy, because it has a good丨rationalized丨plot. The depiction of love aspects, in addition to the final kiss, there is nothing. Columbia is a new company, and I can only consider this product to be a newly emerging comedy with a unique style. Indeed, this film has a very special and novel meaning.

The plot is long and the film is short, so in addition to telling the story, it is difficult to contain a large amount of expression. Jack Holt

Soviet Film "Storm Over Asia" Premieres Today 268

It is now known that the Soviet film "Storm Over Asia," the most famous work of the Soviet Union, will start screening at the Mingzhu Grand Theater on Fusheng Road today. It is rumored that the outside world initially rumored that the film would premiere at the Shanghai Grand Theater. After investigation, this was not true, because the film strongly criticized modern oppressors. The entrance of the theater is right in the concession, and there may be various inconveniences. Therefore, it was decided to arrange it at the Mingzhu Grand Theater in the completely Chinese area for official release. As for the price level, the theater only sells for a small amount of three-fifths of a dollar in order to seek popularity. This is the first time that Soviet films have been sold at such a low price.

The patrolman played by Jock Holt has a complete gentlemanly demeanor, and his silent performance is also top-notch. In the whole film, he is more than capable of being a leader. However, there is nothing particularly exciting, and everyone except him in this film is a supporting role (there is no supporting actor). The performances are generally good, and most of them are extremely humorous characters, which breaks the dullness of "terror."

The light is good. The photography is very mediocre, and many shots are taken from the same position, which is very monotonous. There are countless funny words in the dialogue, so it is not annoying. There is slight noise in the sound, which seems to be a problem with the projector. In terms of technology, the advantage of this film is the tight organization and editing, which adds a lot of horror and jokes, making it more colorful. The setting is ordinary and does not reach the level of mystery and greatness.

The biggest flaw of this film is that the expression is not enough. There are many characters and things that make viewers unable to understand. There are also minor loopholes, such as the scarcity of guns, etc., which need not be discussed in depth.

"A Scene in First Love" will be released at the Paris Grand Theater soon

"White Gold Dragon" Did Not Pass 269

— Mobo Feng

Southern Film Company was founded by Cantonese actor Xue Juexian. The film "White Gold Dragon" commissioned to Tianyi Company has been around for a long time, and the entire film has been completed. It was sent to the Film Censorship Committee for inspection a few days ago. Unexpectedly, it was not approved due to inconsistent language in the film. Now Xue Juexian and his wife Tang Xueqing will return to Guangdong together, so the release of "White Gold Dragon" will be a long way off.

Audience Opinions

Reading "Morning of the Metropolis" and Speaking of "City Nights" 270

— Shadow

Rummaging through a movie special issue from several days ago, I stumbled upon an article that talked about "Morning of the Metropolis" and then went on to "City Nights," which couldn't help but make me smile wryly.

Let's not talk about whether "City Nights" or "Morning of the Metropolis" was a success or failure because! When both films premiered, they both received whole-page criticisms, and the critics and audiences understood very well.

If it weren't for someone as ignorant as Mr. "Wan," then every reader who cares about movies would surely know whether "Morning of the Metropolis" and "City Nights" started filming two or three months apart, and whether "Morning of the Metropolis" stopped filming for several months in between, waiting for "City Nights" to come out so they could imitate it.

Furthermore, the "path of light" in "Morning of the Metropolis" was not clearly implied, while the "path of light" in "City Nights" can only be let Mr. Wan himself "struggle forward" on.

Editor's Note: If Mr. Shadow knows the order in which "City Nights" and "Morning of the Metropolis" were produced and the time between them, he can refute Mr. "Wan's" theory based on facts; but to deem Mr. "Wan" as "ignorant" just because he doesn't know the order in which the film companies produced the two films is extremely uncharitable. Moreover, since we have opened a "Public Opinion" column, it is intended to give movie audiences a place to express their opinions. Opinions vary, and no one should be forced to agree. We hope readers can understand this point and not turn this column into a battlefield. (Unsigned)

Foreword to First Love 271

— Zhang Guan

"First Love" is a valuable work that embodies the true meaning of love. It tells the story of a duke who falls in love with a girlfriend. Later, this girlfriend is torn between two lovers, and the duke is willing to sacrifice himself to show his pure love. Although the plot is simple, it is quite tortuous and interesting. The main actors, Ronald Colman, Merle Oberon, and Josette Day, are all quite successful. The whole play is well-paced and full of interest. It premiered in Paris on the 7th.

Movie Novel Treasure Competition: State Fair (8) 272

— Hui Jun

They left the Ferris wheel, strolling around, seeming not to notice the crowds of people. "What would you like to do now?" Pantoff asked.

"Take me to see your newspaper office," Maggie suggested. Pantoff hesitated, telling her that there were too many colleagues there, which was very inconvenient, making Maggie feel a sudden chill. Didn't he want his friends to see her? she thought.

"I would most like my colleagues to see you!" Pantoff said firmly. "But before we go there, I want you to promise me one thing!"

"What is it?" Maggie asked blankly.

"That is! Tonight or tomorrow, you will marry me," he said. This made Maggie even more confused. She asked him what the reason was. "Because," Pantoff, at least very humbly, said depressingly. "My past life has been too despicable... I never thought I would genuinely treat a woman sincerely... So, Maggie, if they see you with me, they will gossip about you. But if you marry me..."

Maggie stared blankly. It seemed that everything was shrouded in darkness. Finally, she said dejectedly, "I don't think I want to go to the newspaper office anymore. There's probably nothing good to see there."

"Would you like to take a car ride and feel the wind, go to the place where we were last night?" Pantoff forced a smile.

"Okay," Maggie's voice had a hint of bitterness.

In Emeline's bedroom, Wayne and Emeline stood closely embracing each other.

"I still can't believe I've had such an amazing encounter," Wayne said, his arm reaching out to embrace her.

Emeline returned his kiss. Then, deftly, she freed herself from his embrace to turn on the electric light.

"This is our last night, Wayne," she said. There was an irreversible meaning in her tone.

Wayne was suspicious. "You can believe," he protested bravely. "There are still countless sweet nights for us to enjoy in the rest of our lives. You can't think that I'll let you slip away now." Suddenly, Emeline, standing in front of the window, turned her back to him, and he couldn't help but shout, "Why, Emeline? What have I done wrong?" (To be continued)
